(*) This solution though formal ly ac c eptable is undesir able b e c ause one purp ose
of interp olation pr oblems is to include solutions in Gr aÆti as new invariants, [A CC].

T o de/ACne the solution which I found let us c al l a vertex v a divisor of u, if
every neighb or of u is a neighb or of v. The r elation v /AM u i/AB v is a divisor of u is a
quasi-or dering of V - the set of vertic es of G. A subset F of V is a c al le d a filter ,
if for every element v of F, and u, s.t v /AM u, u also b elongs to F.
If F is a principal /AClter of V, i.e, if F is of the form (v) = f u:v /AM u g for
some element v of V, then F is an indep endent subset of G.
Inde e d, let a,b b e elements of F = (v). Neither a nor b ar e adjac ent to v,
b e c ause v /AM a would imply that v is adjac ent to itself. Now, if b wer e adjac ent to a,
v /AM a would imply that v is adjac ent a. Henc e a,b and thus also F ar e indep endent
sets.
If we put now I(G) to b e the numb er of elements of a maximum princip al /AClter
of V, then I satis/ACes al l c onditions of the interp olation pr oblem.
